```

(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(b 6)   (   )---(   )   (b 7)---(   )---(   )---(   )   (   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(b 6)   (b 9)---(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )---(   )   (   )
```
